\index{A\+O\+M\+\_\+\+E\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+O\+PY@{A\+O\+M\+\_\+\+E\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+O\+PY}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}
\paragraph{\texorpdfstring{A\+O\+M\+\_\+\+E\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+O\+PY}{AOM\_EFLAG\_NO\_UPD\_ENTROPY}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define A\+O\+M\+\_\+\+E\+F\+L\+A\+G\+\_\+\+N\+O\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+\_\+\+E\+N\+T\+R\+O\+PY~(1 $<$$<$ 26)}



Disable entropy update. 

When this flag is set, the encoder will not update its internal entropy model based on the entropy of this frame. \mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ga31943c4d9e34f90a0691949109c224fd}\label{group__aom__encoder_ga31943c4d9e34f90a0691949109c224fd}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aac7fbd0de7295387d7821f1889c47790}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aac7fbd0de7295387d7821f1889c47790}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+P\+U\+U\+S\+ED@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+P\+U\+U\+S\+ED}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+P\+U\+U\+S\+ED@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+P\+U\+U\+S\+ED}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5adac09e1a8da079b08fca5ccbf981f1a6}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5adac09e1a8da079b08fca5ccbf981f1a6}} 
A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+P\+U\+U\+S\+ED&Codec control function to set encoder internal speed settings. Changes in this value influences, among others, the encoder\textquotesingle{}s selection of motion estimation methods. Values greater than 0 will increase encoder speed at the expense of quality.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid range\+: 0..8 
\end{DoxyNote}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+N\+T\+I\+Z\+ER@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+N\+T\+I\+Z\+ER}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+N\+T\+I\+Z\+ER@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+A\+S\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+U\+A\+N\+T\+I\+Z\+ER}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5acf37709a88970e0dffb961d951fd43a0}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5acf37709a88970e0dffb961d951fd43a0}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+F\+R\+A\+M\+ES@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+F\+R\+A\+M\+ES}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+F\+R\+A\+M\+ES@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+F\+R\+A\+M\+ES}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a327fb270f37bbb008b0f146542ce7483}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a327fb270f37bbb008b0f146542ce7483}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+N\+G\+TH@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+N\+G\+TH}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+N\+G\+TH@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+R\+N\+R\+\_\+\+S\+T\+R\+E\+N\+G\+TH}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5affd2c213f24a12d13bb51e31be993e60}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5affd2c213f24a12d13bb51e31be993e60}}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+I\+NG@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+I\+NG}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+I\+NG@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+I\+NG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aba539b6646278e7ff40f67f38639d294}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aba539b6646278e7ff40f67f38639d294}} 
A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+I\+NG&Codec control function to set visual tuning. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5af67f265bf63bf8f1268b3a14ae26606c}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5af67f265bf63bf8f1268b3a14ae26606c}} 
A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+EL&Codec control function to set constrained / constant quality level. \begin{DoxyAttention}{Attention}
For this value to be used \hyperlink{structaom__codec__enc__cfg_a3fd74d888658039d09bc4eacf163a495}{aom\+\_\+codec\+\_\+enc\+\_\+cfg\+\_\+t\+::rc\+\_\+end\+\_\+usage} must be set to \hyperlink{group__encoder_gga7c084d3ecef569aad166ce70b0e8a957a70aa1f15e91f6576ba3e63879947be64}{A\+O\+M\+\_\+\+CQ} or \hyperlink{group__encoder_gga7c084d3ecef569aad166ce70b0e8a957aff3bbd4fe870b4b946c2093e59eb14e5}{A\+O\+M\+\_\+Q}. 
\end{DoxyAttention}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid range\+: 0..63 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a9e1965ffa40d2d87556b65748c63adcc}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a9e1965ffa40d2d87556b65748c63adcc}} 
A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT&Codec control function to set Max data rate for Intra frames. This value controls additional clamping on the maximum size of a keyframe. It is expressed as a percentage of the average per-\/frame bitrate, with the special (and default) value 0 meaning unlimited, or no additional clamping beyond the codec\textquotesingle{}s built-\/in algorithm.

For example, to allocate no more than 4.\+5 frames worth of bitrate to a keyframe, set this to 450. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+RS@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+RS}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+RS@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+RS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aef4facbd3745aa7f2a604faaf68316ff}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aef4facbd3745aa7f2a604faaf68316ff}} 
A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+B\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+P\+A\+T\+I\+A\+L\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+RS&Codec control function to set number of spatial layers. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a54b7c950e51f39a3cb7344a2665b9929}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a54b7c950e51f39a3cb7344a2665b9929}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+\_\+\+B\+I\+T\+R\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+P\+CT&Codec control function to set max data rate for Inter frames. This value controls additional clamping on the maximum size of an inter frame. It is expressed as a percentage of the average per-\/frame bitrate, with the special (and default) value 0 meaning unlimited, or no additional clamping beyond the codec\textquotesingle{}s built-\/in algorithm.

For example, to allow no more than 4.\+5 frames worth of bitrate to an inter frame, set this to 450. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+C\+B\+R\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+CT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+C\+B\+R\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+CT}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+C\+B\+R\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+CT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+C\+B\+R\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+CT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ade327180f01d27d22abd94c1f0a8bc9e}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ade327180f01d27d22abd94c1f0a8bc9e}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+C\+B\+R\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+S\+T\+\_\+\+P\+CT&Boost percentage for Golden Frame in C\+BR mode. This value controls the amount of boost given to Golden Frame in C\+BR mode. It is expressed as a percentage of the average per-\/frame bitrate, with the special (and default) value 0 meaning the feature is off, i.\+e., no golden frame boost in C\+BR mode and average bitrate target is used.

For example, to allow 100\% more bits, i.\+e, 2X, in a golden frame than average frame, set this to 100. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+S\+S\+L\+E\+SS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+S\+S\+L\+E\+SS}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+S\+S\+L\+E\+SS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+S\+S\+L\+E\+SS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5afe875c6bb02f236be503c8c7b1f15875}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5afe875c6bb02f236be503c8c7b1f15875}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+L\+O\+S\+S\+L\+E\+SS&Codec control function to set lossless encoding mode. A\+V1 can operate in lossless encoding mode, in which the bitstream produced will be able to decode and reconstruct a perfect copy of input source. This control function provides a mean to switch encoder into lossless coding mode(1) or normal coding mode(0) that may be lossy. 0 = lossy coding mode 1 = lossless coding mode

By default, encoder operates in normal coding mode (maybe lossy). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+W\+\_\+\+MT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+W\+\_\+\+MT}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+W\+\_\+\+MT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+W\+\_\+\+MT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a095d0817d339940aa2578924a840fc84}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a095d0817d339940aa2578924a840fc84}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+O\+W\+\_\+\+MT&control function to enable the row based multi-\/threading of encoder. A value that is equal to 1 indicates that row based multi-\/threading is enabled. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+U\+M\+NS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+U\+M\+NS}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+U\+M\+NS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+U\+M\+NS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5acf4ab1ff2fa8d76a78881ad7f1a1294d}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5acf4ab1ff2fa8d76a78881ad7f1a1294d}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+U\+M\+NS&Codec control function to set number of tile columns. In encoding and decoding, A\+V1 allows an input image frame be partitioned into separate vertical tile columns, which can be encoded or decoded independently. This enables easy implementation of parallel encoding and decoding. The parameter for this control describes the number of tile columns (in log2 units), which has a valid range of \mbox{[}0, 6\mbox{]}\+: 0 = 1 tile column 1 = 2 tile columns 2 = 4 tile columns ..... n = 2$\ast$$\ast$n tile columns

By default, the value is 0, i.\+e. one single column tile for entire image. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+R\+O\+WS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+R\+O\+WS}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+R\+O\+WS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+R\+O\+WS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a57f2f2a54f593b398a5e97db7982f817}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a57f2f2a54f593b398a5e97db7982f817}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+R\+O\+WS&Codec control function to set number of tile rows. In encoding and decoding, A\+V1 allows an input image frame be partitioned into separate horizontal tile rows, which can be encoded or decoded independently. The parameter for this control describes the number of tile rows (in log2 units), which has a valid range of \mbox{[}0, 6\mbox{]}\+: 0 = 1 tile row 1 = 2 tile rows 2 = 4 tile rows ..... n = 2$\ast$$\ast$n tile rows

By default, the value is 0, i.\+e. one single row tile for entire image. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+P\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+EL@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+P\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+EL}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+P\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+EL@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+P\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+EL}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a174ffbc2e91a020a8225900e38894137}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a174ffbc2e91a020a8225900e38894137}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+P\+L\+\_\+\+M\+O\+D\+EL&Codec control function to enable R\+DO modulated by frame temporal dependency. By default, this feature is off. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+L\+L\+E\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+L\+L\+E\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+L\+L\+E\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+L\+L\+E\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a465382b6bbca24467739c3c1b94e6483}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a465382b6bbca24467739c3c1b94e6483}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+L\+L\+E\+L\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG&Codec control function to enable frame parallel decoding feature. A\+V1 has a bitstream feature to reduce decoding dependency between frames by turning off backward update of probability context used in encoding and decoding. This allows staged parallel processing of more than one video frames in the decoder. This control function provides a mean to turn this feature on or off for bitstreams produced by encoder.

By default, this feature is off. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+I\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+I\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+I\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+I\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aa0d049453fced5f8079861b16e356c69}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5aa0d049453fced5f8079861b16e356c69}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+R\+R\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+E\+S\+I\+L\+I\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE&Codec control function to enable error\+\_\+resilient\+\_\+mode. A\+V1 has a bitstream feature to guarantee parseability of a frame by turning on the error\+\_\+resilient\+\_\+decoding mode, even though the reference buffers are unreliable or not received.

By default, this feature is off. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a3ec44c6d8987ca88f8f635b7c098c11e}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a3ec44c6d8987ca88f8f635b7c098c11e}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE&Codec control function to enable s\+\_\+frame\+\_\+mode. A\+V1 has a bitstream feature to designate certain frames as S-\/frames, from where we can switch to a different stream, even though the reference buffers may not be exactly identical.

By default, this feature is off. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a17bd297efc31082157785d68fc5a6067}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a17bd297efc31082157785d68fc5a6067}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE&Codec control function to set adaptive quantization mode. A\+V1 has a segment based feature that allows encoder to adaptively change quantization parameter for each segment within a frame to improve the subjective quality. This control makes encoder operate in one of the several A\+Q\+\_\+modes supported.

By default, encoder operates with A\+Q\+\_\+\+Mode 0(adaptive quantization off). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+I\+O\+D\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+ST@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+I\+O\+D\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+ST}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+I\+O\+D\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+ST@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+I\+O\+D\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+ST}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a737368591a37417b108c0706f7510885}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a737368591a37417b108c0706f7510885}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+P\+E\+R\+I\+O\+D\+I\+C\+\_\+\+B\+O\+O\+ST&Codec control function to enable/disable periodic Q boost. One A\+V1 encoder speed feature is to enable quality boost by lowering frame level Q periodically. This control function provides a mean to turn on/off this feature. 0 = off 1 = on

By default, the encoder is allowed to use this feature for appropriate encoding modes. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+I\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+S\+I\+T\+I\+V\+I\+TY@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+I\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+S\+I\+T\+I\+V\+I\+TY}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+I\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+S\+I\+T\+I\+V\+I\+TY@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+I\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+S\+I\+T\+I\+V\+I\+TY}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a8d415cd6976ea5860206e1d3cd3dd222}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a8d415cd6976ea5860206e1d3cd3dd222}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+O\+I\+S\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+N\+S\+I\+T\+I\+V\+I\+TY&Codec control function to set noise sensitivity. 0\+: off, 1\+: On(\+Y\+Only) \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+NT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+NT}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+NT@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+NT}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a2625f566fd5c2675eb2bcd40af858652}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a2625f566fd5c2675eb2bcd40af858652}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+U\+N\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+NT&Codec control function to set content type. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid parameter range\+: A\+O\+M\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+F\+A\+U\+LT = Regular video content (Default) A\+O\+M\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+T\+E\+N\+T\+\_\+\+S\+C\+R\+E\+EN = Screen capture content 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+D\+F\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+D\+F\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+D\+F\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+D\+F\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a277526a4a9b8c413e870ee17ff986e87}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a277526a4a9b8c413e870ee17ff986e87}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+D\+F\+\_\+\+U\+P\+D\+A\+T\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE&Codec control function to set C\+DF update mode. 0\+: no update 1\+: update on every frame 2\+: selectively update \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+M\+A\+R\+I\+ES@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+M\+A\+R\+I\+ES}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+M\+A\+R\+I\+ES@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+M\+A\+R\+I\+ES}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5af64e990728fe37287bac0874d77b22db}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5af64e990728fe37287bac0874d77b22db}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+P\+R\+I\+M\+A\+R\+I\+ES&Codec control function to set color space info. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid ranges\+: 0..23, default is \char`\"{}\+Unspecified\char`\"{}. 0 = For future use 1 = B\+T.\+709 2 = Unspecified 3 = For future use 4 = B\+T.\+470 System M (historical) 5 = B\+T.\+470 System B, G (historical) 6 = B\+T.\+601 7 = S\+M\+P\+TE 240 8 = Generic film (color filters using illuminant C) 9 = B\+T.\+2020, B\+T.\+2100 10 = S\+M\+P\+TE 428 (C\+IE 1921 X\+YZ) 11 = S\+M\+P\+TE RP 431-\/2 12 = S\+M\+P\+TE EG 432-\/1 13 = For future use (values 13 -\/ 21) 22 = E\+BU Tech. 3213-\/E 23 = For future use 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+A\+C\+T\+E\+R\+I\+S\+T\+I\+CS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+A\+C\+T\+E\+R\+I\+S\+T\+I\+CS}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+A\+C\+T\+E\+R\+I\+S\+T\+I\+CS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+A\+C\+T\+E\+R\+I\+S\+T\+I\+CS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a336fc3607a5987f9077c634f07b3cd53}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a336fc3607a5987f9077c634f07b3cd53}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+R\+A\+N\+S\+F\+E\+R\+\_\+\+C\+H\+A\+R\+A\+C\+T\+E\+R\+I\+S\+T\+I\+CS&Codec control function to set transfer function info. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid ranges\+: 0..19, default is \char`\"{}\+Unspecified\char`\"{}. 0 = For future use 1 = B\+T.\+709 2 = Unspecified 3 = For future use 4 = B\+T.\+470 System M (historical) 5 = B\+T.\+470 System B, G (historical) 6 = B\+T.\+601 7 = S\+M\+P\+TE 240 M 8 = Linear 9 = Logarithmic (100 \+: 1 range) 10 = Logarithmic (100 $\ast$ Sqrt(10) \+: 1 range) 11 = I\+EC 61966-\/2-\/4 12 = B\+T.\+1361 13 = s\+R\+GB or s\+Y\+CC 14 = B\+T.\+2020 10-\/bit systems 15 = B\+T.\+2020 12-\/bit systems 16 = S\+M\+P\+TE ST 2084, I\+TU B\+T.\+2100 PQ 17 = S\+M\+P\+TE ST 428 18 = B\+T.\+2100 H\+LG, A\+R\+IB S\+T\+D-\/\+B67 19 = For future use 
\end{DoxyNote}

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+R\+I\+X\+\_\+\+C\+O\+E\+F\+F\+I\+C\+I\+E\+N\+TS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+R\+I\+X\+\_\+\+C\+O\+E\+F\+F\+I\+C\+I\+E\+N\+TS}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+R\+I\+X\+\_\+\+C\+O\+E\+F\+F\+I\+C\+I\+E\+N\+TS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+R\+I\+X\+\_\+\+C\+O\+E\+F\+F\+I\+C\+I\+E\+N\+TS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a0111ed659d2cd11827ac5cd1f3d774b0}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a0111ed659d2cd11827ac5cd1f3d774b0}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+T\+R\+I\+X\+\_\+\+C\+O\+E\+F\+F\+I\+C\+I\+E\+N\+TS&Codec control function to set transfer function info. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid ranges\+: 0..15, default is \char`\"{}\+Unspecified\char`\"{}. 0 = Identity matrix 1 = B\+T.\+709 2 = Unspecified 3 = For future use 4 = US F\+CC 73.\+628 5 = B\+T.\+470 System B, G (historical) 6 = B\+T.\+601 7 = S\+M\+P\+TE 240 M 8 = Y\+Cg\+Co 9 = B\+T.\+2020 non-\/constant luminance, B\+T.\+2100 Y\+Cb\+Cr 10 = B\+T.\+2020 constant luminance 11 = S\+M\+P\+TE ST 2085 Y\+Dz\+Dx 12 = Chromaticity-\/derived non-\/constant luminance 13 = Chromaticity-\/derived constant luminance 14 = B\+T.\+2100 I\+Ct\+Cp 15 = For future use 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+R\+O\+M\+A\+\_\+\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+T\+I\+ON@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+R\+O\+M\+A\+\_\+\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+T\+I\+ON}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+R\+O\+M\+A\+\_\+\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+T\+I\+ON@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+R\+O\+M\+A\+\_\+\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+T\+I\+ON}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5abc5bb5cf57ba1a1193a0593225e881ff}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5abc5bb5cf57ba1a1193a0593225e881ff}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+H\+R\+O\+M\+A\+\_\+\+S\+A\+M\+P\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+O\+S\+I\+T\+I\+ON&Codec control function to set chroma 4\+:2\+:0 sample position info. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid ranges\+: 0..3, default is \char`\"{}\+U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N\char`\"{}. 0 = U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+WN, 1 = V\+E\+R\+T\+I\+C\+AL 2 = C\+O\+L\+O\+C\+A\+T\+ED 3 = R\+E\+S\+E\+R\+V\+ED 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a31bcfcb7057884ceb831146c90086ddd}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a31bcfcb7057884ceb831146c90086ddd}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL&Codec control function to set minimum interval between G\+F/\+A\+RF frames. By default the value is set as 4. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a0355cea227ab76f9bd77028a39bbfca8}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a0355cea227ab76f9bd77028a39bbfca8}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+G\+F\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+E\+R\+V\+AL&Codec control function to set minimum interval between G\+F/\+A\+RF frames. By default the value is set as 16. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+E\+M\+AP@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+E\+M\+AP}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+E\+M\+AP@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+E\+M\+AP}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a65f19811dc9057230d991647fac243b0}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a65f19811dc9057230d991647fac243b0}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+C\+T\+I\+V\+E\+M\+AP&Codec control function to get an Active map back from the encoder. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a29aa5b07bbdbdc90d7ddb148403b00ad}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a29aa5b07bbdbdc90d7ddb148403b00ad}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+C\+O\+L\+O\+R\+\_\+\+R\+A\+N\+GE&Codec control function to set color range bit. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid ranges\+: 0..1, default is 0 0 = Limited range (16..235 or H\+BD equivalent) 1 = Full range (0..255 or H\+BD equivalent) 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a7d462f767d5feea411c70229a3d39508}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a7d462f767d5feea411c70229a3d39508}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+R\+E\+N\+D\+E\+R\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE&Codec control function to set intended rendering image size. By default, this is identical to the image size in pixels. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5abc032ee5a8dc3f51ab88b64737590f1b}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5abc032ee5a8dc3f51ab88b64737590f1b}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+A\+R\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX&Control to set target sequence level index for a certain operating point(\+O\+P). Possible values are in the form of \char`\"{}\+A\+Bxy\char`\"{}(pad leading zeros if less than 4 digits). AB\+: OP index. xy\+: Target level index for the OP. Can be values 0$\sim$23(corresponding to level 2.\+0 $\sim$ 7.\+3) or 24(keep level stats only for level monitoring) or 31(maximum level parameter, no level-\/based constraints). E.\+g. \char`\"{}0\char`\"{} means target level index 0 for the 0th OP; \char`\"{}111\char`\"{} means target level index 11 for the 1st OP; \char`\"{}1021\char`\"{} means target level index 21 for the 10th OP. If the target level is not specified for an OP, the maximum level parameter of 31 is used as default. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a726d36bbaf587cf30eb263e48a1c2e46}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a726d36bbaf587cf30eb263e48a1c2e46}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+G\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+E\+Q\+\_\+\+L\+E\+V\+E\+L\+\_\+\+I\+DX&Codec control function to get sequence level index for each operating point. There can be at most 32 operating points. The results will be written into a provided integer array of sufficient size. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a8854a06c62269e866d6bac0f3a2e3dc2}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a8854a06c62269e866d6bac0f3a2e3dc2}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+B\+L\+O\+C\+K\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE&Codec control function to set intended superblock size. By default, the superblock size is determined separately for each frame by the encoder.

Experiment\+: E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+I\+T\+I\+ON \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+W\+D\+R\+EF@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+W\+D\+R\+EF}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+W\+D\+R\+EF@{A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+W\+D\+R\+EF}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ac03aab2de7167facffff4e22e8f89687}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ac03aab2de7167facffff4e22e8f89687}} 
A\+O\+M\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+A\+U\+T\+O\+B\+W\+D\+R\+EF&Codec control function to enable automatic set and use bwd-\/pred frames. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+D\+EF@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+D\+EF}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+D\+EF@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+D\+EF}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a6879fe104e23de00f034ed11eb605031}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a6879fe104e23de00f034ed11eb605031}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+D\+EF&Codec control function to encode with C\+D\+EF. C\+D\+EF is the constrained directional enhancement filter which is an in-\/loop filter aiming to remove coding artifacts 0 = do not apply C\+D\+EF 1 = apply C\+D\+EF

By default, the encoder applies C\+D\+EF.

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+QM@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+QM}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+QM@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+QM}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ae63993934cdc5aa36efeec4df87a577e}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ae63993934cdc5aa36efeec4df87a577e}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+QM&Codec control function to encode with quantisation matrices. A\+OM can operate with default quantisation matrices dependent on quantisation level and block type. 0 = do not use quantisation matrices 1 = use quantisation matrices

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+M\+\_\+\+M\+IN@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+M\+\_\+\+M\+IN}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+M\+\_\+\+M\+IN@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+M\+\_\+\+M\+IN}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ae611944ba148b6446d4387dd9b452917}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ae611944ba148b6446d4387dd9b452917}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+Q\+M\+\_\+\+M\+IN&Codec control function to set the min quant matrix flatness. A\+OM can operate with different ranges of quantisation matrices. As quantisation levels increase, the matrices get flatter. This control sets the minimum level of flatness from which the matrices are determined.

By default, the encoder sets this minimum at half the available range.

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+8\+X8@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+8\+X8}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+8\+X8@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+8\+X8}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a7ef16c780349c5fee8281f1e5b4a6718}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a7ef16c780349c5fee8281f1e5b4a6718}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+I\+S\+T\+\_\+8\+X8&Codec control function to encode with dist\+\_\+8x8. The dist\+\_\+8x8 is enabled automatically for model tuning parameters that require measuring distortion at the 8x8 level. This control also allows measuring distortion at the 8x8 level for other tuning options (e.\+g., P\+S\+NR), for testing purposes. 0 = do not use dist\+\_\+8x8 1 = use dist\+\_\+8x8

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+TG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+TG}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+TG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+TG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a9ac0044ad63e6848a482db04f0858c44}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a9ac0044ad63e6848a482db04f0858c44}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+N\+U\+M\+\_\+\+TG&Codec control function to set a maximum number of tile groups. This will set the maximum number of tile groups. This will be overridden if an M\+TU size is set. The default value is 1.

Experiment\+: T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+PS \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+TU@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+TU}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+TU@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+TU}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a353037d84b6c47ac0138fa843b70a2bb}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a353037d84b6c47ac0138fa843b70a2bb}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+TU&Codec control function to set an M\+TU size for a tile group. This will set the maximum number of bytes in a tile group. This can be exceeded only if a single tile is larger than this amount.

By default, the value is 0, in which case a fixed number of tile groups is used.

Experiment\+: T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+G\+R\+O\+U\+PS \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+S\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+G2@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+S\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+G2}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+S\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+G2@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+S\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+G2}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a12575637cfea2f096a3f403933389979}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a12575637cfea2f096a3f403933389979}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+A\+N\+S\+\_\+\+W\+I\+N\+D\+O\+W\+\_\+\+S\+I\+Z\+E\+\_\+\+L\+O\+G2&Codec control function to set the number of symbols in an A\+NS data window. The number of A\+NS symbols (both boolean and non-\/booleans alphabets) in an A\+NS data window is set to 1 $<$$<$ value.

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid range\+: \mbox{[}8, 23\mbox{]}
\end{DoxyNote}

A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+T\+I\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE&Codec control function to set min partition size. This will set min partition size. The default value is 4 for 4x4. valid values are \mbox{[}4, 8, 16, 32, 64, 128\mbox{]} min\+\_\+partition\+\_\+size is applied to both width and height of the partition. i.\+e, both width and height of a partition can not be smaller than the min\+\_\+partition\+\_\+size, except the partition at the picture boundary. \\

A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+M\+O\+O\+T\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA&Codec control function to turn on / off smooth intra modes usage. This will enable or disable usage of smooth, smooth\+\_\+h and smooth\+\_\+v intra modes. The default value is 1. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a25f7c646aaec0702964c1fb1bf16e298}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a25f7c646aaec0702964c1fb1bf16e298}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+E\+T\+H\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA&Codec control function to turn on / off Paeth intra mode usage. This will enable or disable usage of Paeth intra mode. The default value is 1. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+F\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+F\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+F\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+F\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a993e0e437aa0d152fe654ba0ab46f9d2}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a993e0e437aa0d152fe654ba0ab46f9d2}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+C\+F\+L\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+RA&Codec control function to turn on / off C\+FL uv intra mode usage. This will enable or disable usage of chroma-\/from-\/luma intra mode. The default value is 1. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+R\+ES@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+R\+ES}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+R\+ES@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+R\+ES}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a86e399de03aa825bb7e594e3df1bf71b}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a86e399de03aa825bb7e594e3df1bf71b}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+R\+ES&Codec control function to turn on / off frame superresolution. This will enable or disable frame superresolution. The default value is 1 If A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+S\+U\+P\+E\+R\+R\+ES is 0, then this flag is forced to 0. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+L\+E\+T\+TE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+L\+E\+T\+TE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+L\+E\+T\+TE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+L\+E\+T\+TE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a98d0e84130317b6c072c2deac106dede}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a98d0e84130317b6c072c2deac106dede}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+P\+A\+L\+E\+T\+TE&Codec control function to turn on/off palette mode. \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+BC@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+BC}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+BC@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+BC}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a3e59c51f12c7350fee92c1c0d4901ab0}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a3e59c51f12c7350fee92c1c0d4901ab0}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+I\+N\+T\+R\+A\+BC&Codec control function to turn on/off intra block copy mode. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+TA@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+TA}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+TA@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+TA}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a3155057080db493c868eb2d42d435b61}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a3155057080db493c868eb2d42d435b61}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+A\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+TA&Codec control function to turn on/off intra angle delta. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ad26eda6211bf3d5fe4f5999ec52b264b}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ad26eda6211bf3d5fe4f5999ec52b264b}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE&Codec control function to set the delta q mode. A\+V1 supports a delta q mode feature, that allows modulating q per superblock. This control makes encoder operate in one of several D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+\_\+\+Q\+\_\+modes supported\+: 0\+: Not Supported 1\+: Use modulation to maximize objective quality 2\+: Use modulation to maximize perceptual quality

By default, encoder operates with D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+Q\+\_\+\+Mode 0(deltaq signaling off). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+L\+F\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+L\+F\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+L\+F\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+L\+F\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ab2d0e42bcf19974859e61d8709c5ae09}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ab2d0e42bcf19974859e61d8709c5ae09}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+D\+E\+L\+T\+A\+L\+F\+\_\+\+M\+O\+DE&Codec control function to turn on/off loopfilter modulation when delta q modulation is enabled. Note A\+V1 only supports loopfilter modulation when delta q modulation is enabled as well. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5af341538631ffe2ac2b562c8b5336a10a}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5af341538631ffe2ac2b562c8b5336a10a}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+I\+N\+G\+L\+E\+\_\+\+T\+I\+L\+E\+\_\+\+D\+E\+C\+O\+D\+I\+NG&Codec control function to set the single tile decoding mode to 0 or 1. 0 means that the single tile decoding is off, and 1 means that the single tile decoding is on.

Experiment\+: E\+X\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+LE \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+ST@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+ST}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+ST@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+ST}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a0c45a2184ff7068f470cb9f128c3605d}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a0c45a2184ff7068f470cb9f128c3605d}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+E\+N\+A\+B\+L\+E\+\_\+\+M\+O\+T\+I\+O\+N\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+O\+R\+\_\+\+U\+N\+I\+T\+\_\+\+T\+E\+ST&Codec control function to enable the extreme motion vector unit test in A\+V1. Please note that this is only used in motion vector unit test. 0 \+: off, 1 \+: M\+A\+X\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+E\+M\+E\+\_\+\+MV, 2 \+: M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+E\+X\+T\+R\+E\+M\+E\+\_\+\+MV \\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a857e822046c62a4c774b1d16c4e453dd}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a857e822046c62a4c774b1d16c4e453dd}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+M\+I\+N\+G\+\_\+\+I\+N\+F\+O\+\_\+\+T\+Y\+PE&Codec control function to signal picture timing info in the bitstream. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid ranges\+: 0..1, default is \char`\"{}\+U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+W\+N\char`\"{}. 0 = U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+WN, 1 = E\+Q\+U\+AL 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+OR@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+OR}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+OR@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+OR}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a437e6b282a2395b4b08a9acde3e41cfb}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a437e6b282a2395b4b08a9acde3e41cfb}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+E\+S\+T\+\_\+\+V\+E\+C\+T\+OR&Codec control function to add film grain parameters (one of several preset types) info in the bitstream. \begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
Valid ranges\+: 0..11, default is \char`\"{}0\char`\"{}. 0 = U\+N\+K\+N\+O\+WN, 1..16 = different test vectors for grain 
\end{DoxyNote}
\\

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+A\+B\+LE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+A\+B\+LE}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+A\+B\+LE@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+A\+B\+LE}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ad5846c6f49d37e65a03c39e68d487097}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5ad5846c6f49d37e65a03c39e68d487097}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+F\+I\+L\+M\+\_\+\+G\+R\+A\+I\+N\+\_\+\+T\+A\+B\+LE&Codec control function to set the path to the film grain parameters. \\

A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+T\+I\+E\+R\+\_\+\+M\+A\+SK&Control to set bit mask that specifies which tier each of the 32 possible operating points conforms to. Bit value 0\+: Main Tier; 1\+: High Tier. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+CR@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+CR}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+CR@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+CR}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5afe2dd2cf29cc6202786ecbf132288d99}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5afe2dd2cf29cc6202786ecbf132288d99}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+M\+I\+N\+\_\+\+CR&Control to set minimum compression ratio. Take integer values. If non-\/zero, encoder will try to keep the compression ratio of each frame to be higher than the given value divided by 100. E.\+g. 850 means minimum compression ratio of 8.\+5. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a1d968f9cc0ad869e36680328b0badaf7}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a1d968f9cc0ad869e36680328b0badaf7}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+L\+A\+Y\+E\+R\+\_\+\+ID&Codec control function to set the layer id. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+MS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+MS}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+MS@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+MS}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a94c12c49cd70d86651136ec37230d719}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a94c12c49cd70d86651136ec37230d719}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+P\+A\+R\+A\+MS&Codec control function to set S\+VC paramaeters. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG}!A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}}\index{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder@{A\+O\+Media A\+O\+M/\+A\+V1 Encoder}!A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG@{A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG}}}\mbox{\Hypertarget{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a24a2e10051709d0684d8b7acfbf988c9}\label{group__aom__encoder_ggae78dde67a6d78f332e9bdba0dde42db5a24a2e10051709d0684d8b7acfbf988c9}} 
A\+V1\+E\+\_\+\+S\+E\+T\+\_\+\+S\+V\+C\+\_\+\+R\+E\+F\+\_\+\+F\+R\+A\+M\+E\+\_\+\+C\+O\+N\+F\+IG&Codec control function to set reference frame config\+: the ref\+\_\+idx and the refresh flags for each buffer slot. \\
\hline
